SELECT CASE
    WHEN [f].[UserId1] = @__userId_0 THEN [u].[username]
    ELSE [u0].[username]
END AS [username], CASE
    WHEN [f].[UserId1] = @__userId_0 THEN [u].[avatar_url]
    ELSE [u0].[avatar_url]
END AS [avatar], CASE
    WHEN [f].[UserId1] = @__userId_0 THEN [u].[id]
    ELSE [u0].[id]

    ELSE [u0].[id]

    ELSE [u0].[username]
